     <p> Coniferous trees shroud the trail, snowy boughs creaking beneath the weight of their wintery burden. A single post marks a fork in the ancient road, the signage weathered beyond legibility. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('mH618BGC');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Several caravans are circling a large camp fire on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail.
